1. Executive Summary
This report presents findings from a comprehensive UAT exercise on the Student Info module of 
Eskoolia
 School ERP. The module was tested across 8 sub-modules covering students, categories, groups, guardians, promotions, documents, transfers, multi-class records, and attendance. A total of 71 test cases were executed spanning CRUD operations, input validation, security/permissions, and UI/UX evaluation across 15 UI pages.

1.2 Critical Findings
ZERO Permission Enforcement (P0): 
All 10 security tests returned CRITICAL. A teacher with 0 permissions can READ all 797 student records, CREATE new students, DELETE student records, CREATE categories, and MARK attendance for any student. This is the same systemic vulnerability found in Role Permission and Admin Section modules.
Duplicate Key Returns 500 (P1): 
Three separate duplicate scenarios return 500: duplicate 
admission_no
 on students, duplicate category name, and duplicate attendance (same 
student+date
). All should return 400 with validation messages. Pattern is systemic across the entire ERP.
XSS Vulnerability - HTML Stored in Names (P1): 
HTML tags like <b>Bold</b> and <script> are accepted and stored in student 
first_name
 fields. The Student List UI renders these without sanitization. If the 
frontend
 does not escape HTML, this enables stored XSS attacks where malicious scripts execute for every user viewing the student list.
Student Export Shows Only 25 of 797 (P1): 
The Student Export page shows 'Total students ready for export: 25' when there are 797 students in the system. The export function only processes the first page of paginated results, silently dropping 97% of student data.
Section Dropdown Not Filtered by Class (P2): 
On Multi Class, Delete Record, Disabled Students, and Promote pages, the Section dropdown shows ALL 25 sections from ALL 12 
classes instead of filtering by the selected class. Users see 12 'A' options and 12 'B' options with no way to distinguish 
which
 belongs to which class.
2. Module Architecture
2.1 API Endpoints Tested
Base URL: http://187.127.137.154/api/v1/students/

4. Bug Summary & Priority Matrix
4.1 P0 - Critical (Blocker)
BUG-S001: Zero Permission Enforcement on Student APIs
Any authenticated user (teacher, driver, student) can READ all student records, CREATE new students, DELETE students, CREATE categories/groups, and MARK attendance. The custom permission model from access-control is completely unenforced on student and attendance APIs.
Impact: Complete PII breach. Student personal data (name, DOB, gender, blood group, guardian info, address) 
accessible
 to all users. A disgruntled teacher could delete all student records or mark false attendance.
Fix: Same as Admin Section - implement custom DRF permission class checking role permissions from 
access_control
 tables. Apply globally.
4.2 P1 - High
BUG-S002: Duplicate 
admission_no
 Returns 500
Creating a student with an existing 
admission_no
 returns HTTP 500. The 
IntegrityError
 from the database unique constraint bubbles up unhandled. 
Should
 return 400 with '
admission_
no
 already exists' message.
BUG-S003: Duplicate Category Name Returns 500
Same pattern as BUG-S002. Adding 
unique_together
 or serializer-level validation would fix both.
BUG-S004: Duplicate Attendance Returns 500
Creating attendance for the same 
student+date
 combination returns 500 instead of 400. Should enforce 
unique_together
 on (student, 
attendance_date
) and return a clear validation message.
BUG-S005: XSS - HTML Tags Stored and Rendered in Student Names
The API accepts HTML/script tags in 
first_name
 and 
last_name
 fields. The Student List page renders these without HTML escaping. This enables stored XSS attacks where any user creating a student with malicious name content can execute scripts on every user viewing the student list.
Fix: Server-side input sanitization (strip HTML tags from name fields) AND frontend output escaping (React auto-escapes by default unless using 
dangerouslySetInnerHTML
).
BUG-S006: Student Export Only Exports 25 of 797 Records
The export page only processes the first page of paginated API results. It shows 'Total students ready for export: 25' when there are 797 students. Schools relying on this for data backup or reporting would lose 97% of their data.
Fix: The export function must fetch ALL pages or use a dedicated export API endpoint that returns unpaginated results.
BUG-S007: FK Constraint Error on Student Delete (500)
Deleting a student who has attendance, marks, or fee records returns 500 Internal Server Error. Should return 400/409 with message: 'Cannot delete student with existing attendance/marks/fee records. Archive the student instead.'
4.3 P2 - Medium
BUG-S008: Section Dropdown Shows All Sections (Not Filtered by Class)
On Multi Class, Delete Record, Disabled Students, and Promote pages, the section dropdown loads ALL 25 sections from every class. Users see 12 identical 'A' options and 12 identical 'B' options with no way to distinguish them. Fix: Filter sections by selected class using dependent dropdown.
BUG-S009: Class 2 Missing value Attribute in Dropdowns
The option element for Class 2 in all class dropdowns has no value attribute, while all other classes (1, 3-12) do. This could cause Class 2 selections to fail silently.
BUG-S010: Future DOB and Future Attendance Date Accepted
A student with 
date_of_birth
 = 2030-01-01 is accepted. Attendance for 2027-01-01 is also accepted. Both need date range validation.
BUG-S011: Promote Page - Target Year Shows Only Past Years
The 'Select Academic Year' dropdown for promotion target only shows 2025-2026 and 2024-2025. Since promotions move students forward, the current/next academic year should be available.
BUG-S012: Subject Attendance API Not Implemented
The /attendance/subject-attendance/ endpoint returns 404. The UI page exists at /attendance/subject but has no backing REST API. Same for attendance import.
BUG-S013: SMS Sending Time Page Not Implemented
Page shows placeholder text: 'This Student Info screen is now routed correctly. Legacy parity UI for this page can be implemented next.' Should be either implemented or hidden from navigation.
BUG-S014: Typo - '
Scholership
' in Category Dropdown
The student category dropdown shows '
Scholership
' instead of 'Scholarship'. Data-level fix required in admin-setup.
5. Improvement Recommendations
5.1 Immediate Fixes (Sprint 1)
Implement Permission Middleware: 
Create a custom DRF permission class (HasModulePermission) that intercepts every 
ViewSet
 action and checks the user role permissions. This is the same fix needed for Admin Section and ALL other modules. Should be implemented ONCE as 
a global
 middleware.
Add Input Sanitization: 
Strip HTML tags from all text input fields (
first_name
, 
last_name
, etc.) at the serializer level. Use bleach or 
django
-bleach library. Additionally verify the frontend escapes output properly (React JSX auto-
escapes, but
 check for 
dangerouslySetInnerHTML
 usage).
Fix Duplicate Key Error Handling Globally: 
Add a global DRF exception handler that catches 
IntegrityError
 and returns 400 with a descriptive message. This single fix resolves BUG-S002, S003, S004, and all similar bugs across every module.
Fix Student Export Pagination: 
The export function must iterate through ALL API pages or use an unpaginated endpoint. 
Currently
 silently dropping 97% of student data.
5.2 Short-term Improvements (Sprint 2-3)
Implement Dependent Dropdowns: 
When a class is selected, filter the section dropdown to show only sections belonging to that class. Use an API call like /sections/?
class_id
=X or filter client-side from a class-section mapping object.
Add Date Range Validation: 
DOB must 
be
 in the past (and reasonable: 3-20 years 
ago
 for school students). Attendance date must be today or in the past, within the current academic year. Promotion target year must be current or future.
Implement Soft Delete for Students: 
Instead of hard delete (which fails due to FK constraints), implement soft delete (
is_active
=false, 
is_deleted
=true) with an archive workflow. Students with related data should be archived, not deleted. The 'Disabled Students' page already exists for this purpose.
Register Missing API Endpoints: 
Add subject-attendance, attendance-import, and attendance report endpoints to the REST router. Currently the UI pages exist but use internal 
routes
 not available via standard API.
Add Server-Side Pagination with Page Controls: 
The student list loads 
all 797
 records at once. As the school grows to 2000+ students, this will cause severe performance issues. Implement server-side pagination with page controls (page size, next/previous, total count).
Guardian Module Integration: 
The guardian API shows 0 records despite the Add Student form having a guardian section. The form creates 
guardians
 but they are not properly linked to the student records via the API. Verify the guardian FK relationship is working.
6. AI Integration Strategy
If Claude were building this Student Module to world-class standards, here is how AI would transform it from a basic CRUD system into an intelligent student management platform.
6.1 Smart Enrollment & Admission
Admission Prediction: 
ML model predicts admission likelihood based on inquiry source, class demand, category distribution, and historical conversion rates. Auto-prioritizes high-probability leads 
for
 follow-up.
Document Verification: 
AI-powered OCR extracts data from uploaded birth certificates, transfer certificates, and report cards. Auto-fills student fields (name, DOB, previous school) and flags discrepancies between uploaded documents and manual entry.
6.2 Attendance Intelligence
Absence Pattern Detection: 
AI identifies chronic absenteeism patterns: students with 3+ consecutive absences, declining attendance trends, day-of-week patterns (always absent on Mondays), and seasonal drops. Sends early warning alerts to class teachers and parents.
Dropout Risk Scoring: 
Combines attendance data with academic performance, fee payment history, and behavioral records to generate a dropout risk score (0-100) for each student. Students above threshold get flagged for counselor intervention.
6.3 Academic Performance Prediction
Grade Prediction: 
Based on attendance patterns, assignment submissions, test scores, and historical data, AI predicts which students are at risk of failing upcoming exams. Provides actionable recommendations: 'Ravi needs 15 extra hours of Math tutoring based on his Unit Test 2 performance.'
Learning Gap Analysis: 
AI analyzes subject-wise attendance and exam results to identify topic-level gaps. Generates personalized study plans: 'Section 9A has 60% proficiency in Quadratic Equations vs 85% school average - recommend 3 additional sessions.'
6.4 Smart Promotion & Placement
Promotion Readiness Score: 
AI generates a multi-factor promotion readiness score combining attendance (>75% required), exam results (passing in all subjects), behavioral record (no serious incidents), and fee clearance. Automates bulk promotion for qualifying students.
Section Balancing: 
When promoting students to the next class, AI optimally distributes them across sections to balance gender ratio, academic performance mix, and special needs distribution. Prevents the common problem of one section being significantly stronger than others.
6.5 Parent Communication AI
Automated SMS/Notification: 
AI drafts personalized absence notifications: 'Dear Mr. Reddy, Aarav was absent today (March 28). He has been absent 3 days this month. Please contact the class teacher if he is unwell.' Supports multilingual (English, Hindi, Telugu).
Progress Report Generation: 
AI generates natural language progress summaries from structured data: 'Priya has shown excellent improvement in 
Science
 (from 72% to 88%) but needs attention in Mathematics (declined from 65% to 58%). Her attendance is 92%
 which
 is above 
class average
.'
6.6 Data Quality & Integrity
Duplicate Detection: 
Fuzzy matching algorithm identifies potential duplicate students based on name similarity, DOB, parent name, and phone number. Flags 'Aadhya Boya (ADM3542)' and 'Aadhya Boya (ADM3758)' as potential duplicates for review.
Data Completeness Scoring: 
AI scores each student profile on completeness (0-100%). Currently: 
blood_group
 is empty for most students, category is null for many, guardian is null for all 797. Dashboard shows 'Data completeness: 45% - 797 students missing guardian info.'
6.7 Cross-Module Intelligence Dashboard
Student 360 View: 
Single page showing all data for a student: attendance trend chart, exam results timeline, fee payment status, behavioral incidents, transport route, and AI-generated insights. Teachers see this before parent-teacher meetings.
Class Health Dashboard: 
AI-generated class-level metrics: average attendance, grade distribution, at-risk student count, fee collection rate. Principals see all classes 
at a glance
 with red/yellow/green indicators.
7. Claude-Level Standard vs Current State

8. Conclusion
The Student Info module passed 42 of 71 test cases (59% pass rate). The 10 CRITICAL security findings and multiple P1 bugs (XSS vulnerability, broken export, duplicate key errors) make this module unsafe for production use.
The core CRUD operations work correctly for students, categories, and groups. The UI is comprehensive with 15 pages covering enrollment, attendance, promotion, and export workflows. However, the security vulnerability (zero permission enforcement) combined with the XSS vulnerability creates a dangerous combination: any authenticated user can inject malicious scripts into student names that would execute for every admin viewing the student list.
The Student Export bug silently dropping 97% of data is a critical data integrity issue. Schools relying on the export function for backup, reporting, or regulatory compliance would receive incomplete data without any warning.
The AI integration strategy in Section 6 would transform this module from basic data entry into an intelligent student management platform with dropout prediction, attendance intelligence, automated parent communication, and data quality management. The immediate priority must be fixing the security and XSS vulnerabilities.
Recommended Action: 
DO NOT 
deploy to
 production until (1) permission enforcement middleware is implemented globally, (2) HTML input sanitization is added, and (3) student export pagination is fixed. All other improvements can follow in subsequent sprints.
